       <article class="content-wrapper wrapper clearfix detail-block-md" id="article-32226">
        <header class="content-header">
         <h1>
          Yankees Warn Eduardo Nunez To Stop Showing Up Derek Jeter By Making Routine Plays At Shortstop
         </h1>
        </header>
        <main class="content-body large-thing" data-area="Article Body">
         <div class="content-masthead">
          <figure class="content-image on-trigger-overlay">
           <div class="image" data-image-id="21824" data-type="image">
            <div>
            </div>
            <noscript>
             <img src="http://i.onionstatic.com/onion/2182/4/16x9/600.jpg"/>
            </noscript>
           </div>
          </figure>
          <div class="on-overlay on-overlay-scale">
           <button class="on-overlay-close" type="button">
            Close
           </button>
           <figure class="content-image">
            <div class="image" data-image-id="21824" data-type="image">
             <div>
             </div>
             <noscript>
              <img src="http://i.onionstatic.com/onion/2182/4/16x9/600.jpg"/>
             </noscript>
            </div>
           </figure>
          </div>
         </div>
         <div class="content-meta small-thing">
          <div>
           <a class="content-type" data-track-action="Meta: Feature Type" data-track-category="Article" data-track-label="/search?tags=" href="/features/sports-news-in-brief">
            SPORTS NEWS IN BRIEF
           </a>
           <span class="content-published">
            April 27, 2013
           </span>
          </div>
          <div>
           <span class="content-issue">
            <a data-track-action="Meta: Issue" data-track-category="Article" data-track-label="/issue/4917/" href="/issue/4917/">
             Vol 49 Issue 17
            </a>
            <span class="bul">
             
            </span>
           </span>
           <span class="content-tags">
            <a data-track-action="Meta: Tags" data-track-category="Article" data-track-label="/tag/sports" href="/tag/sports">
             Sports
            </a>
            <span class="bul">
             
            </span>
            <a data-track-action="Meta: Tags" data-track-category="Article" data-track-label="/tag/baseball" href="/tag/baseball">
             Baseball
            </a>
           </span>
          </div>
          <div class="article-share-tools share-container">
           <div class="share-tools share-widget" data-share-description="NEW YORKMultiple reports from within the New York Yankees clubhouse confirmed Saturday that team officials have warned shortstop Eduardo Nunez to stop showing up injured team captain Derek Jeter by making routine plays in the field and at the plate..." data-share-image="http://i.onionstatic.com/onion/2182/4/16x9/1200.jpg" data-share-redirect-url="http://www.theonion.com/fb-close" data-share-title="Yankees Warn Eduardo Nunez To Stop Showing Up Derek Jeter By Making Routine Plays At Shortstop" data-share-url="http://www.theonion.com/r/32226">
            <a class="share-facebook button" data-action="Facebook share clicked" data-track-action="Meta: Share" data-track-category="Article" data-track-label="Facebook" href="#" target="_blank" title="Share via Facebook">
             <i class="fa fa-facebook fa-fw">
             </i>
            </a>
            <a class="share-twitter button" data-action="Twitter share clicked" data-track-action="Meta: Share" data-track-category="Article" data-track-label="Twitter" href="#" title="Share via Twitter">
             <i class="fa fa-twitter fa-fw">
             </i>
            </a>
            <a class="share-mail button" data-action="Email share clicked" data-track-action="Meta: Share" data-track-category="Article" data-track-label="Email" href="#" title="Share via Email">
             <i class="fa fa-envelope fa-fw">
             </i>
            </a>
           </div>
          </div>
          <div class="dfp dfp-slot-article-button" data-ad-unit="article-button" data-targeting='{"dfp_pagetype": "article", "dfp_content_id": 32226}'>
          </div>
         </div>
         <div class="large-thing content-main">
          <div class="content-text">
           <div>
            <p>
             NEW YORKMultiple reports from within the New York Yankees clubhouse confirmed Saturday that team officials have warned shortstop Eduardo Nunez to stop showing up injured team captain Derek Jeter by making routine plays in the field and at the plate. Every cleanly fielded ground ball sends a pretty strong message that Eduardo is trying to upstage Derek, said Yankees manager Joe Girardi, who blasted Nunez for having the audacity to turn a double play without a throwing error, claiming the commonplace display of physical capabilities clearly reminds fans of Jeters advancing age and declining skills. He needs to just cut it out; hes making Derek look bad. Last week, when Eduardo legged out an infield single, that was like a direct slap in the face to our team captain. Girardi, however, lauded third baseman Kevin Youkilis for helping everybody forget that Alex Rodriguez is still on the team.
            </p>
           </div>
          </div>
